Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And if the dislocation is on the side, it must not be stretched downward or lifted from the ground, but should be positioned as if the hip were dislocated to the side, as we have said regarding lying on the two hips; and place it under its fold, and stretch the ligament as we have said before, and must press on the joint at the table; it will be right when the patient extends his legs, and they are equal; then adjust the thighs, and apply the plaster and the bandage, so that the hips do not move; and let it rest for three or four days, then remove it, and apply the plaster again; and if you see that they are equal, stretch it as before, and leave it for three days; then remove it, and let the hip go well, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knee can be dislocated in three ways: namely, inward and outward, and behind; and it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the signs are such that you command the patient to bend his leg at the thigh, and if it does not sit at the thigh, know that it is dislocated; and the restoration of all this is that you make the patient sit straight, extend his leg if he can, and place your back against his thigh, and put his foot on yours; then take his knee with both palms, and pull between them, then bend the two sides of the knee firmly; and have other ministers extend his foot, until the knee returns to its place, and the signs are that his leg sits lightly at the thigh; and apply the plaster, and heat the leg to the thigh, and bind them together strongly for three or four days, then release the bindings; and do not allow the patient to work much until the limb is strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not properly aligned, administer strong stretching, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation from the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heel is dislocated once, and fully reset both inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and protrudes forward to the part where it was dislocated: the resetting is light, and one should gently stretch it with their hands when it is only dislocated.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is fully dislocated, you must seat the patient upright, and hold them by the ministers outside at the leg, above the ankle; then pull the foot toward yourself with your right hand, and twice with your left, then stretch it upwards, and firmly place the foot upward; do this twice as we have said, by pulling and pulling the foot; if it returns, that is good; if not, reattempt the procedure, for it will return; and if it cannot return thus, make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and drive a stake firmly into the earth between their thighs, binding the stake with bandages tightly so as not to displace the patient; then hold the thigh by the ministers, and another minister stretch the foot at their hands or at the stake, tying it above the ankle; then stretch each minister equally, and the stake should remain between the patient's thighs to hold the patient when stretched; finally, place your fingers evenly at the dislocation and have another minister hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is in place, put the plaster and stops on it, and strengthen the bandage, and tie the foot to the leg, and guard the nerves which are behind the ankle, that the ligatures be not too tight; then let it remain for two or three days, and when the ligatures soften, so does the bandage; then loosen them on the third or fourth day, and prevent the patient from walking for four days; and if he goes before this term is completed, it is not safety that he will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if abscesses come about, you must soothe them, as we have said elsewhere, until they are healed.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the shoulders are dislocated, it is necessary to extend them beautifully with effort, and this is a light matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any notch of the back or hip bone, you must seat the patient on a firm surface or on a bench completely straight, and place his foot over what is revealed by these joints, then press firmly on his foot until it returns; and when it is equal, and nothing is revealed, then put a shoulder table under the sole of the foot, then extract it firmly, and let him rest for three days, then release him; and let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with dislocation, and one sees hope for recovery: do not be presumptuous in the treatment, if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it long, and if you are not patient, merciful, and slow; nor too bold. At the beginning of things, use cooling remedies to pacify hot abscesses, and leave the patient under God's care if there is no hope of recovery; and when there is hope, immediately set the limb in place as the abscesses cool down. When the limb is in place, administer cooling remedies for abscesses, and treat the wound as it should be with ointments that dry out the area; and if with dislocation there are fractures or small broken bones, remove them, and do what we have said in simple diseases; and guard against entering a path of fear, according to what I have said, for this will bring you misfortune according to your Creator, and for the wisdom that arms and protects you.
Amen	Amen
